{com}.         
.         local prepRaw = 0
{txt}
{com}.         local prepDec = 0
{txt}
{com}.         local prepDummies = 0
{txt}
{com}.         local prepDecDummies = 0
{txt}
{com}.         local gapReg = 0
{txt}
{com}.         local doGraph = 0
{txt}
{com}.         local gapGraph = 0
{txt}
{com}.         local tabReg = 1
{txt}
{com}.         local bwReg     = 0
{txt}
{com}.         
. /********************************
> * 2. Data Setup (Percentiles)   *
> ********************************/
.         if `prepRaw' {c -(}
.                         
.                         use `data'/IPUMS-USA_Extension-correct.dta, clear
.                         
.                         keep if inlist(year,1980,1990,2000,2010,2019)
.                 
.                         gen rent_inc = 100*rentgrs/(inctot/12) if inctot>0
.                         gen hval_inc = valueh/(inctot/12) if inctot>0
.                         
.                         
.                         gen inc_month = inctot/12
.                         gen own100 = 100*(1-renter)
.                         
.                         //compute percentiles
.                         local vars "rentgrs valueh own100 inc_month"
.                         
.                         levelsof year, local(years)
.                         
.                         foreach v of local vars {c -(}
{txt}  2{com}.                                 di "computing percentiles for `v'..."
{txt}  3{com}.                                 gen pctr_`v'=.
{txt}  4{com}.                                 foreach y of local years {c -(}
{txt}  5{com}.                                         di "    year=`y'..."
{txt}  6{com}.                                         xtile pctr_`v'_`y' = `v' [aw=hhwt] if year==`y', nq(100)
{txt}  7{com}.                                         replace pctr_`v'=pctr_`v'_`y' if year==`y'
{txt}  8{com}.                                 {c )-}
{txt}  9{com}.                                 
.                                 
.                         {c )-}
.                         
.                 
.                         
.                         save "`data'/fig2data.dta", replace
.                 
.                 {c )-}
{txt}
{com}. /********************************
> * 2. Data Setup (Deciles)       *
> ********************************/
.         if `prepDec' {c -(}
.                 
.                 use `data'/IPUMS-USA_Extension-correct.dta, clear
.                         
.                         keep if inlist(year,1980,1990,2000,2010,2019)
.                         
.                         
.                 
.                         gen rent_inc = 100*rentgrs/(inctot/12) if inctot>0
.                         gen hval_inc = valueh/(inctot/12) if inctot>0
.                         
.                         
.                         gen inc_month = inctot/12
.                         gen own100 = 100*(1-renter)
.                 
.                         //compute deciles       
.                         local vars "rentgrs valueh own100 inc_month"
.                         
.                         levelsof year, local(years)
.                         
.                         foreach v of local vars {c -(}
{txt}  2{com}.                                 di "computing deciles for `v'..."
{txt}  3{com}.                                 gen dec_`v'=.
{txt}  4{com}.                                 foreach y of local years {c -(}
{txt}  5{com}.                                         di "    year=`y'..."
{txt}  6{com}.                                         xtile dec_`v'_`y' = `v' [aw=hhwt] if year==`y', nq(10)
{txt}  7{com}.                                         replace dec_`v'=dec_`v'_`y' if year==`y'
{txt}  8{com}.                                 {c )-}
{txt}  9{com}.                                 
.                                 
.                         {c )-}
.                         
.                         
.                         save "`data'/tab1data.dta", replace
.         {c )-}
{txt}
{com}. /********************************
> * 3. Prep Dummies (Percentiles) *
> ********************************/               
.                 
. if `prepDummies' {c -(}
.                 
.                 use "`data'/fig2data.dta", clear
.                 
.                 
.                 local races "asian chinese japanese korean vietnamese filipino indian black"
.                         levelsof pctr_inc_month, local(ps)
.                         foreach p of local ps {c -(}
{txt}  2{com}.                                  
.                                 di "p=`p'"
{txt}  3{com}.                                 //generate dummy for income ranks
.                                         gen _incr_p`p' = 0 if pctr_inc_month!=.
{txt}  4{com}.                                         replace _incr_p`p' = 1 if pctr_inc_month==`p'
{txt}  5{com}.                                 foreach r of local races {c -(}
{txt}  6{com}.                                         di "race=`r'..."
{txt}  7{com}.                                 //generate interaction with race
.                                         gen _ia_`r'_incr_p`p' = `r'*_incr_p`p'
{txt}  8{com}.                                 
.                                 
.                                 {c )-}
{txt}  9{com}.                 
.                         {c )-}
.                         
.                         
.                         save "`data'/fig2_reg_data.dta", replace
.                         
.                 {c )-}
{txt}
{com}. /********************************
> * 3. Prep Dummies (Deciles)     *
> ********************************/               
.                 
. if `prepDecDummies' {c -(}
.                 
.                 use "`data'/tab1data.dta", clear
.                 
.                         local races "asian chinese japanese korean vietnamese filipino indian black"
.                 
.                         levelsof dec_inc_month, local(ds)
.                         foreach d of local ds {c -(}
{txt}  2{com}.                                  
.                                 di "d=`d'"
{txt}  3{com}.                                 //generate dummy for income ranks
.                                         gen _incr_d`d' = 0 if dec_inc_month!=.
{txt}  4{com}.                                         replace _incr_d`d' = 1 if dec_inc_month==`d'
{txt}  5{com}.                                 foreach r of local races {c -(}
{txt}  6{com}.                                         di "race =`r'"
{txt}  7{com}.                                 //generate interaction with asian
.                                         gen _ia_`r'_incr_d`d' = `r'*_incr_d`d'
{txt}  8{com}.                                 
.                                 {c )-}
{txt}  9{com}.                         {c )-}
.                         
.                         
.                         save "`data'/tab1_reg_data.dta", replace
.                         
.                 {c )-}
{txt}
{com}.                 
. 
. /********************************
> * 4. Gap Regressions            *
> ********************************/
. if `gapReg'{c -(}
.                 use `data'/fig2_reg_data.dta
.                 local races "asian chinese japanese korean vietnamese filipino indian black"
.                 foreach r of local races {c -(}
{txt}  2{com}.                 //create interactions
.                         gen _ia_`r'_y = `r'*pctr_inc_month
{txt}  3{com}.                 
.                 //run regression for each year and outcome
.                         
.                         
.                         local vars "rentgrs valueh own100"
{txt}  4{com}.                         local controls "educ age sex hhtype farm metarea statefip"
{txt}  5{com}.                         local years "1980,1990,2000,2010,2019"
{txt}  6{com}.                         
.                         sum `controls'
{txt}  7{com}.                 
.                         replace pctr_own100=own100 //this one is a linear probability model (no rank necessary)
{txt}  8{com}.                         levelsof year, local(years) //grab available years
{txt}  9{com}.                         foreach v of local vars {c -(}
{txt} 10{com}.                                 gen `r'_rgap_`v'_p25=.
{txt} 11{com}.                                 gen `r'_rgap_`v'_p50=.
{txt} 12{com}.                                 gen `r'_rgap_`v'_p75=.
{txt} 13{com}.                                 foreach y of local years {c -(}
{txt} 14{com}.                         
.                                         //run parametric regression (linear in income rank)
.                                                 reg pctr_`v' pctr_inc_month `r' _ia_`r'_y `controls' [aw=hhwt] if year==`y', 
{txt} 15{com}.                                         
.                                         //predice race gap at various income ranks
.                                                 replace `r'_rgap_`v'_p25 = _b[`r'] + _b[_ia_`r'_y]*25 if year==`y'
{txt} 16{com}.                                                 replace `r'_rgap_`v'_p50 = _b[`r'] + _b[_ia_`r'_y]*50 if year==`y'
{txt} 17{com}.                                                 replace `r'_rgap_`v'_p75 = _b[`r'] + _b[_ia_`r'_y]*75 if year==`y'
{txt} 18{com}.                                 {c )-}
{txt} 19{com}.                                 
.                         {c )-}
{txt} 20{com}.                 {c )-}
.                                         save `data'/graph.dta, replace
.         {c )-}       
{txt}
{com}. /********************************
> * 5. Graphing                   *
> ********************************/       
. if `doGraph' {c -(}
.                 use `data'/graph.dta, clear
.                 local races "asian chinese japanese korean vietnamese filipino indian black"
.                 foreach r of local races {c -(}
{txt}  2{com}.                         preserve
{txt}  3{com}.                         //collapse saved coefficients by year
.                                 collapse `r'_rgap*, by(year)
{txt}  4{com}.                 
.                         //plot saved coefficients
.                                 tsset year
{txt}  5{com}.                         
.                         
.                                 graph drop _all
{txt}  6{com}.                 
.                                 local vars "rentgrs valueh own100"
{txt}  7{com}.                                 foreach v of local vars {c -(}
{txt}  8{com}.                                 
.                                         if "`v'"=="rentgrs" {c -(}
{txt}  9{com}.                                                 local ylab "`r'/Non-`r' Rent Rank Gap"
{txt} 10{com}.                                         {c )-}
{txt} 11{com}.                                         else if "`v'"=="valueh" {c -(}
{txt} 12{com}.                                                 local ylab "`r'/Non-`r' House Price Rank Gap"
{txt} 13{com}.                                         {c )-}
{txt} 14{com}.                                         else if "`v'"=="own100" {c -(}
{txt} 15{com}.                                                 local ylab "`r'/Non-`r' Ownership Gap (perc. pt.)"
{txt} 16{com}.                                         {c )-}
{txt} 17{com}.                                 
.                                 #delimit ;
{txt}delimiter now ;
{com}.                                         tsline `r'_rgap_`v'_p25 `r'_rgap_`v'_p50 `r'_rgap_`v'_p75,
>                                 
>                                         lwidth(thin thick thin)
>                                         lpattern(dash solid solid)
>                                 
>                                         legend(ring(0) pos(5) col(1) region(style(none)) order(1 "25-th Perc. Inc. Rank" 2 "50-th Perc. Inc. Rank" 3 "75-th Perc. Inc. Rank"))
>                                 
>                                         xlabel(1980(10)2020, grid gstyle(major) glstyle(dot) glcolor(black) glwidth(small))
>                                         ylabel(-20(5)20, grid gstyle(major) glstyle(dot) glcolor(black) glwidth(small))
>                                         yline(0,lcolor(black) lwidth(thin))
>                                 
>                                         ytitle("`ylab'")
>                                         xtitle("Year")
>                                 
>                                 
>                                         name(`r'_`v')
>                                 
>                                         ;
{txt} 18{com}.                                 #delimit cr
{txt}delimiter now cr
{com}.                                         graph export "`output'/`r'_extended_rgap_`v'.pdf", as(pdf) name(`r'_`v') replace
{txt} 19{com}.                                 {c )-}
{txt} 20{com}.                                 restore
{txt} 21{com}.                         {c )-}
.                 {c )-}
{txt}
{com}. 
. /********************************
> * 1980 Gap Graphics             *
> ********************************/
.         if `gapGraph' {c -(} 
.                 use `data'/IPUMS-USA_Extension-correct.dta, clear
.                 
.                 local races "asian chinese japanese korean vietnamese indian filipino black"
.                 foreach r of local races{c -(}
{txt}  2{com}.                         preserve
{txt}  3{com}.                                 drop if year!=1980
{txt}  4{com}.                                 
.                                 gen rent_inc = 100*rentgrs/(inctot/12) if inctot>0
{txt}  5{com}.                                 gen hval_inc = valueh/(inctot/12) if inctot>0
{txt}  6{com}.                         
.                                 xtile rentp = rentgrs [aw=hhwt], nq(100)
{txt}  7{com}.                                 xtile valuep = valueh [aw=hhwt], nq(100)
{txt}  8{com}.                                 xtile incp = inctot [aw=hhwt], nq(100)
{txt}  9{com}.                                 
.                                 gen `r'_b = incp if `r'==1
{txt} 10{com}.                                 
.                                 reg rentp i.`r'_b
{txt} 11{com}.                                 
.                                 //2a, 2c, 2e
.                                 
.                                 #delimit ;
{txt}delimiter now ;
{com}.                                 binscatter rentp incp [aw=hhwt],
>                                 by(`r') nq(50)
>                                 linetype(qfit)
>                                 name(`r'_Fig2a,replace)
>                                 title("Rent Rank Gap in 1980")
>                                 ytitle("Rent Rank")
>                                 xtitle("Income Rank")
>                                 legend(ring(0) pos(1) col(1))
>                                 ;
{txt} 12{com}.                                 #delimit cr
{txt}delimiter now cr
{com}.                                 graph export `output'/`r'_2a.pdf, as(pdf) name(`r'_Fig2a) replace
{txt} 13{com}.                                 
.                                 #delimit
{txt}delimiter now ;
{com}.                                 binscatter valuep incp [aw=hhwt],
>                                 by(`r') nq(50)
>                                 linetype(qfit)
>                                 name(`r'_Fig2c,replace)
>                                 title("House Price Rank Gap in 1980")
>                                 ytitle("Price Rank")
>                                 xtitle("Income Rank")
>                                 legend (ring(0) pos(1) col(1))
>                                 ;
{txt} 14{com}.                                 #delimit cr
{txt}delimiter now cr
{com}.                                 graph export `output'/`r'_2c.pdf, as(pdf) name(`r'_Fig2c) replace
{txt} 15{com}.                                 
.                                 gen own100 = 100*(1-renter)
{txt} 16{com}.                                 
.                                 #delimit ;
{txt}delimiter now ;
{com}.                                 binscatter own100 incp [aw=hhwt],
>                                 by(`r') nq(50)
>                                 linetype(qfit)
>                                 name(`r'_Fig2e,replace)
>                                 title("Ownership Rate Gaps in 1980")
>                                 ytitle("Ownership Rate")
>                                 xtitle("Income Rank")
>                                 legend (ring(0) pos(1) col(1))
>                                 ;
{txt} 17{com}.                                 #delimit cr
{txt}delimiter now cr
{com}.                                 graph export `output'/`r'_2e.pdf, as(pdf) name(`r'_Fig2e) replace
{txt} 18{com}.                         restore 
{txt} 19{com}.                 {c )-}
.         {c )-}               
{txt}
{com}. /********************************
> * Table 1 Regressions           *
> ********************************/
.         if `tabReg' {c -(}           
.                 clear
.                 use `data'/tab1_reg_data.dta
.                                 
.                 drop _incr_d1
.                 
.                 //by year: summ newrooms yrbuilt black _incr_d* educ age sex hhtype farm metro statefip
.                 
.                 /*local controls "educ age sex hhtype farm metro statefip"
>                 local early "1970"
>                 foreach e of local early {c -(}
>                         di "Year = `e'"
>                         reg yrbuilt black _incr_d* `controls' if year==`e'
>                         reg newrooms black _incr_d* `controls' if year==`e'
>                 {c )-}*/
.                 
.                 
.                 local races "asian chinese japanese korean vietnamese filipino indian black"
.                 local controls2 "educ age sex hhtype farm metro metarea statefip"
.                 local years "1980 1990 2000 2010 2019"
.                 foreach r of local races {c -(}
{txt}  2{com}.                         foreach y of local years {c -(}
{txt}  3{com}.                                 di "Year = `y'"
{txt}  4{com}.                                 reg yrbuilt `r' _incr_d* `controls2' if year==`y'
{txt}  5{com}.                                 reg newrooms `r' _incr_d* `controls2' if year==`y'
{txt}  6{com}.                         {c )-}
{txt}  7{com}.                 {c )-}

{com}. 
. /********************************
> * Between Race Regressions      *
> ********************************/       
.         if `bwReg' {c -(}
.                 clear
.                 use `data'/tab1_reg_data.dta
.                 
.                 drop _incr_d1
.                 
.                 local races "asian chinese japanese korean vietnamese filipino indian black"
.                 local controls2 "educ age sex hhtype farm metro metarea statefip"
.                 local years "1980 1990 2000 2010 2019"
.                 foreach r of local races {c -(}
{txt}  2{com}.                         foreach y of local years {c -(}
{txt}  3{com}.                                 di "Year = `y'"
{txt}  4{com}.                                 reg yrbuilt asian _incr_d* `controls2' if year==`y' & asian==1 | `r'== 1
{txt}  5{com}.                                 reg newrooms asian _incr_d* `controls2' if year==`y' & asian==1 | `r'== 1
{txt}  6{com}.                         {c )-}
{txt}  7{com}.                 {c )-}
.                 foreach r of local races {c -(}
{txt}  2{com}.                         foreach y of local years {c -(}
